[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability has been detected in the libexif library [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring fuzzing operations. The overflow occurs when reading [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m byte from a [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheap-allocated buffer, specifically during the processing of Fuji makernote data in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mEXIF parsing. The issue is triggered in the `exif_get_slong` function while [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempting to read beyond the bounds of a [0m[1;36m56[0m[39m-byte allocated region.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability, specifically a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte read operation [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat accesses memory [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes beyond the end of an allocated [0m[1;36m56[0m[39m-byte heap region. [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer has assigned this a SCARINESS score of [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m, indicating a moderate [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mseverity issue.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Issue Details[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability manifests during the execution of the `exif_from_data_fuzzer` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith the following characteristics:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Error Location:**[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overflow occurs at address `[0m[1;36m0x50600000011f[0m[39m`, which is [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes after the end [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof a [0m[1;36m56[0m[39m-byte region allocated at `[0m[1;36m0x5060000000e0[0m[39m` to `[0m[1;36m0x506000000118[0m[39m`[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The read operation attempts to access [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m byte beyond the valid memory region[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Call Stack Analysis:**[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability is triggered through the following execution path:[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` - The fuzzer entry point[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. `exif_data_new_from_data` - Creates EXIF data structure from input[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. `exif_data_load_data` - Loads and processes EXIF data[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. `exif_mnote_data_fuji_load` - Processes Fuji-specific makernote data[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. `exif_get_long` - Retrieves a long integer value[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. `exif_get_slong` - The actual location where the overflow occurs at line [0m[1;36m137[0m[39m, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcharacter [0m[1;36m36[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Observations[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Vendor-Specific Code:** The issue occurs specifically in Fuji makernote data [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`exif_mnote_data_fuji_load`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, suggesting that the vulnerability may be [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrelated to handling manufacturer-specific EXIF extensions.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Data Extraction Functions:** The problem manifests in utility functions [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`exif_get_slong` and `exif_get_long`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that are responsible for extracting numeric [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalues from binary data, indicating potential issues with bounds checking during [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata parsing.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Memory Allocation:** The [0m[1;36m56[0m[39m-byte buffer was allocated through the standard [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`malloc` pathway, suggesting the allocation itself succeeded but the subsequent [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maccess pattern exceeded the buffer boundaries.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Deduplication Token:** The dedup token [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_get_slong--exif_get_long--exif_mnote_data_fuji_load` indicates this is a [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munique issue in this specific code path.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Areas for Investigation[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo obtain a holistic understanding of this vulnerability, the following components [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould be investigated:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **exif-utils.c [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m137[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:** The specific location where `exif_get_slong` reads [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeyond buffer boundaries. The implementation of both `exif_get_slong` and [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_get_long` functions should be examined for proper bounds checking.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **exif-mnote-data-fuji.c [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m175[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:** The Fuji makernote data loading function [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhere `exif_get_long` is called. This should be reviewed to understand how buffer [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msizes are calculated and validated before passing data to utility functions.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **exif-data.c:** [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m1025[0m[39m: The `exif_data_load_data` function which orchestrates the data [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mloading process[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m159[0m[39m: The `exif_data_new_from_data` function which initializes the EXIF [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata structure[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Buffer Size Calculation:** Investigation is needed into how the [0m[1;36m56[0m[39m-byte buffer[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize was determined and whether the Fuji makernote data processing correctly [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maccounts for the actual data requirements.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Endianness Handling:** Since `exif_get_slong` and `exif_get_long` are [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvolved, the byte order conversion logic should be examined to ensure it doesn't [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minadvertently cause out-of-bounds reads.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibexif/fuji/exif-mnote-data-fuji.[0m[1;92mc:206[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m220[0m                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mn->order[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter analyzing the code snippets and the evaluation report, I have identified the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mroot cause of the heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability in the Fuji makernote data [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability occurs in `libexif/fuji/exif-mnote-data-fuji.c` at line [0m[1;36m175[0m[39m, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhere `exif_get_long` is called without an immediate bounds check:[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdatao += exif_get_long [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf + datao + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, EXIF_BYTE_ORDER_INTEL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe function reads [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes from position `buf + datao + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich equals `buf + [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mn->offset + [0m[1;36m14[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. While there is a bounds check at line [0m[1;36m166[0m[39m that validates [0m[1;36m18[0m[39m bytes[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare available from `n->offset`, this early validation violates the defensive [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprogramming pattern consistently used throughout the libexif codebase.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue is that:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The check at line [0m[1;36m166[0m[39m happens before `datao` is computed[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. There's no immediate validation before the actual read operation at line [0m[1;36m175[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. This violates the established pattern where bounds checks occur immediately [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore each read operation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mas seen in Canon, Pentax, and main exif-data.c [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementations[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Evidence from Code Analysis[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Correct Pattern [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexif-data.[0m[1;92mc:426[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m431[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: Checks `[0m[1;35mCHECKOVERFLOW[0m[1;39m([0m[39moffset, ds, [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimmediately before calling `exif_get_short`[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Correct Pattern [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfuji own co[0m[1;92mde:210[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m220[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: Checks `[0m[1;35mCHECKOVERFLOW[0m[1;39m([0m[39mo, buf_size, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m12[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` before reading entry data with multiple `exif_get_*` calls[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Similar Vulnerability in Olympus [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m385[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: The Olympus implementation has [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe same pattern where `exif_get_long` is called after offset modifications without[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mre-checking bounds[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Critical Logic to Preserve[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The Fuji makernote format structure: [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m-byte header + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte offset field + IFD [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffset value[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The byte order must remain INTEL[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The `datao` calculation logic that adds the offset value to locate the IFD[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All subsequent entry parsing logic must remain unchanged[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix: Add Bounds Check Before exif_get_long Call in Fuji Implementation[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: `libexif/fuji/exif-mnote-data-fuji.[0m[1;92mc:175[0m[39m`[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Implementation Steps**:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Add an explicit `CHECKOVERFLOW` validation immediately before the [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_get_long` call at line [0m[1;36m175[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The check should validate that [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes are available at position `datao + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m`[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. If the check fails, log a corruption error and return early[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. This follows the defensive programming pattern established throughout the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcodebase[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Code Change Pattern**:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m After line [0m[1;36m173[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mn->order = EXIF_BYTE_ORDER_INTEL;[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Before line [0m[1;36m175[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdatao += [0m[1;35mexif_get_long[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mCHECKOVERFLOW[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdatao + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, buf_size, [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    exif_log [0m[1;39m([0m[39men->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_CORRUPT_DATA,[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[32m"ExifMnoteDataFuji"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"Short MakerNote"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return;[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdatao += exif_get_long [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf + datao + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, EXIF_BYTE_ORDER_INTEL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Justification[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Follows Established Pattern**: This matches the pattern used throughout the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcodebase where bounds checks occur immediately before read operations [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexif-data.[0m[1;92mc:426[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m431[0m[39m, fuji:[0m[1;36m210[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m214[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Defensive Programming**: Even though the check at line [0m[1;36m166[0m[39m should [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtheoretically cover this range, adding an explicit check before the read operation [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprovides defense-in-depth[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Minimal Impact**: This change only adds validation; it doesn't modify the core[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic or data processing flow[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Consistency**: Makes the Fuji implementation consistent with other makernote [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementations [0m[1;39m([0m[39mCanon, Pentax[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that check bounds immediately before reads[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Preserves Functionality**: All valid inputs that currently work will continue [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto work; only malformed/malicious inputs that would cause buffer overflows will be [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrejected[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Side Effects**:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Some malformed EXIF files that previously processed [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincorrectly[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m may now be [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrejected[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This is actually a positive side effect, as these files were triggering undefined[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Mitigation**:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fix only affects error cases, not normal processing[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The error handling follows the existing pattern [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlog and return[0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to valid data processing paths[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is Optimal[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Surgical Fix**: Changes only the vulnerable code path without affecting other [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Pattern Compliance**: Aligns with the codebase's established defensive [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprogramming practices[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **No External Dependencies**: Doesn't modify utility functions or break [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minterfaces[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Test Compatible**: Doesn't change the API or behavior for valid inputs, so [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting tests should pass[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Future-Proof**: Prevents similar issues if the code is modified in the future[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
